# This file contains certain basic analysis for the best performance

### separate CCDS and normal parameters
```
b = ['AAA', 'ALX1', 'BBB', 'CCDC85A', 'CCDS47813.1', 'CCDS9942.1', 'CDH20', 'CDH9', 'CLEC14A']
b = b*10

def two(a):
  l1 = l2 = []
  for i in a:
    if i[:4].upper() == "CCDS":
      l2.append(i)
    else:
      l1.append(i)
  return l1,l2

def ttt(a):
  l1 = [x for x in a if x[:4].upper() == "CCDS"]
  l2 = [x for x in a if x not in l1]
  return l1,l2

def tttt(a):
  l1 = [x for x in a if x[:4].upper() == "CCDS"]
  l2 = set(a) - set(l1)
  return l1, list(l2)

def tttt_(a):
  l1 = set([x for x in a if x[:4].upper() == "CCDS"])
  l2 = set(a) - set(l1)
  return list(l1), list(l2)

def ttttt(a):
  l1 = list(filter(lambda x: x[:4].upper() == "CCDS", a))
  l2 = set(a) - set(l1)
  return l1, list(l2)

In [11]: timeit two(b)
22.6 µs ± 1.53 µs per loop (mean ± std. dev. of 7 runs, 10000 loops each)

In [12]: timeit ttt(b)
35.7 µs ± 3.11 µs per loop (mean ± std. dev. of 7 runs, 10000 loops each)

In [13]: timeit tttt(b)
18.1 µs ± 802 ns per loop (mean ± std. dev. of 7 runs, 100000 loops each)

In [14]: timeit tttt_(b)
17.6 µs ± 327 ns per loop (mean ± std. dev. of 7 runs, 100000 loops each)

In [15]: timeit ttttt(b)
23.7 µs ± 1.21 µs per loop (mean ± std. dev. of 7 runs, 10000 loops each)
 ```

def get_kws(keywords):
    keywords_CCDS = set([x for x in keywords if x[:4].upper() == "CCDS"])
    keywords_GS = list(set(keywords) - keywords_CCDS)
    keywords_CCDS = list(keywords_CCDS)
    return keywords_GS, keywords_CCDS
def get_result(keywords_GS,keywords_CCDS):
    results = Crispr.objects.filter(Q(ccds_id__in=keywords_CCDS) | Q    (gene__in=keywords_GS))
    return results
def find_info(keywords_GS,keywords_CCDS):
    found_info = {"hit":[], "miss":[]}
    for kw in keywords_GS:
        if results.filter(gene=kw).exists():
            found_info['hit'].append(kw)
            continue
        found_info['miss'].append(kw)
    for kw in keywords_CCDS:
        if results.filter(ccds_id=kw).exists():
            found_info['hit'].append(kw)
            continue
        found_info['miss'].append(kw)
    return found_info

keywords_GS, keywords_CCDS = get_kws(all_genes)

In [14]: timeit get_kws(all_genes)
7.06 ms ± 9.45 µs per loop (mean ± std. dev. of 7 runs, 100 loops each)

results = get_result(keywords_GS,keywords_CCDS)

In [20]: timeit get_result(keywords_GS,keywords_CCDS)
38.3 ms ± 106 µs per loop (mean ± std. dev. of 7 runs, 10 loops each)

found_info = find_info(keywords_GS,keywords_CCDS)

df = read_frame(results, fieldnames=INCLUDE_LIST)

timeit read_frame(results, fieldnames=INCLUDE_LIST)
585 ms ± 1.54 ms per loop (mean ± std. dev. of 7 runs, 1 loop each)
